alt=\"Hugging Face Spaces\" data-canonical-src=\"https://img.shields.io/badge/%F0%9F%A4%97%20Hugging%20Face-Spaces-blue\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd alt=\"YouTube\" data-canonical-src=\"https://badges.aleen42.com/src/youtube.svg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://arxiv.org/abs/2110.06864\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003earXiv 2110.06864\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIntegrated to \u003ca href=\"https://huggingface.co/spaces\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eHuggingface Spaces\u003c/a\u003e with \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/gradio-app/gradio\"\u003eGradio\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eAbstract\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-abstract\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Abstract\" href=\"#abstract\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eMulti-object tracking (MOT) aims at estimating bounding boxes and identities of objects in videos. Most methods obtain identities by associating detection boxes whose scores are higher than a threshold. The objects with low detection scores, e.g. occluded objects, are simply thrown away, which brings non-negligible true object missing and fragmented trajectories. To solve this problem, we present a simple, effective and generic association method, tracking by associating every detection box instead of only the high score ones. For the low score detection boxes, we utilize their similarities with tracklets to recover true objects and filter out the background detections. When applied to 9 different state-of-the-art trackers, our method achieves consistent improvement on IDF1 scores ranging from 1 to 10 points. To put forwards the state-of-the-art performance of MOT, we design a simple and strong tracker, named ByteTrack. For the first time, we achieve 80.3 MOTA, 77.3 IDF1 and 63.1 HOTA on the test set of MOT17 with 30 FPS running speed on a single V100 GPU.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp align=\"center\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/assets/teasing.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/ifzhang/ByteTrack/raw/main/assets/teasing.png\" width=\"400\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eNews\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-news\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: News\" href=\"#news\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">ByteTrack is a simple, fast and strong multi-object tracker.</h4><a id="user-content-bytetrack-is-a-simple-fast-and-strong-multi-object-tracker" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ByteTrack is a simple, fast and strong multi-object tracker." href="#bytetrack-is-a-simple-fast-and-strong-multi-object-tracker"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Abstract</h2><a id="user-content-abstract" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Abstract" href="#abstract"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Multi-object tracking (MOT) aims at estimating bounding boxes and identities of objects in videos. Most methods obtain identities by associating detection boxes whose scores are higher than a threshold. The objects with low detection scores, e.g. occluded objects, are simply thrown away, which brings non-negligible true object missing and fragmented trajectories. To solve this problem, we present a simple, effective and generic association method, tracking by associating every detection box instead of only the high score ones. For the low score detection boxes, we utilize their similarities with tracklets to recover true objects and filter out the background detections. When applied to 9 different state-of-the-art trackers, our method achieves consistent improvement on IDF1 scores ranging from 1 to 10 points. To put forwards the state-of-the-art performance of MOT, we design a simple and strong tracker, named ByteTrack. For the first time, we achieve 80.3 MOTA, 77.3 IDF1 and 63.1 HOTA on the test set of MOT17 with 30 FPS running speed on a single V100 GPU.</p>
<p align="center" dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/assets/teasing.png"><img src="/ifzhang/ByteTrack/raw/main/assets/teasing.png" width="400" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Installing on the host machine</h3><a id="user-content-1-installing-on-the-host-machine" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Installing on the host machine" href="#1-installing-on-the-host-machine"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Step1. Install ByteTrack.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack.git
cd ByteTrack
pip3 install -r requirements.txt
python3 setup.py develop"><pre>git clone https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack.git
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> ByteTrack
pip3 install -r requirements.txt
python3 setup.py develop</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Step2. Install <a href="https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi">pycocotools</a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip3 install cython; pip3 install 'git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI'"><pre>pip3 install cython<span class="pl-k">;</span> pip3 install <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Step3. Others</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip3 install cython_bbox"><pre>pip3 install cython_bbox</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Docker build</h3><a id="user-content-2-docker-build" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Docker build" href="#2-docker-build"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker build -t bytetrack:latest .

# Startup sample
mkdir -p pretrained &amp;&amp; \
mkdir -p YOLOX_outputs &amp;&amp; \
xhost +local: &amp;&amp; \
docker run --gpus all -it --rm \
-v $PWD/pretrained:/workspace/ByteTrack/pretrained \
-v $PWD/datasets:/workspace/ByteTrack/datasets \

--net=host \

--privileged \
bytetrack:latest"><pre>docker build -t bytetrack:latest <span class="pl-c1">.</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Data preparation</h2><a id="user-content-data-preparation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Data preparation" href="#data-preparation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Download <a href="https://motchallenge.net/" rel="nofollow">MOT17</a>, <a href="https://motchallenge.net/" rel="nofollow">MOT20</a>, <a href="https://www.crowdhuman.org/" rel="nofollow">CrowdHuman</a>, <a href="https://github.com/Zhongdao/Towards-Realtime-MOT/blob/master/DATASET_ZOO.md">Cityperson</a>, <a href="https://github.com/Zhongdao/Towards-Realtime-MOT/blob/master/DATASET_ZOO.md">ETHZ</a> and put them under &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;/datasets in the following structure:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="datasets
   |mot
   |        train
   |        test
   crowdhuman
   |         Crowdhuman_train
   |         Crowdhuman_val
   |         annotation_train.odgt
   |         annotation_val.odgt
   MOT20
   |        train
   |        test
   Cityscapes
   |        images
   |        labels_with_ids
   ETHZ
            eth01
            ...
            eth07"><pre class="notranslate"><code>datasets
   |mot
   |        train
   |        test
   crowdhuman
   |         Crowdhuman_train
   |         Crowdhuman_val
   |         annotation_train.odgt
   |         annotation_val.odgt
   MOT20
   |        train
   |        test
   Cityscapes
   |        images
   |        labels_with_ids
   ETHZ
            eth01
            ...
            eth07
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Then, you need to turn the datasets to COCO format and mix different training data:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/convert_mot17_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_mot20_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_crowdhuman_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_cityperson_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_ethz_to_coco.py"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/convert_mot17_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_mot20_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_crowdhuman_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_cityperson_to_coco.py
python3 tools/convert_ethz_to_coco.py</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Before mixing different datasets, you need to follow the operations in <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/c116dfc746f9ebe07d419caa8acba9b3acfa79a6/tools/mix_data_ablation.py#L6">mix_xxx.py</a> to create a data folder and link. Finally, you can mix the training data:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/mix_data_ablation.py
python3 tools/mix_data_test_mot17.py
python3 tools/mix_data_test_mot20.py"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/mix_data_ablation.py
python3 tools/mix_data_test_mot17.py
python3 tools/mix_data_test_mot20.py</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Model zoo</h2><a id="user-content-model-zoo" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Model zoo" href="#model-zoo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Training</h2><a id="user-content-training" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Training" href="#training"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The COCO pretrained YOLOX model can be downloaded from their <a href="https://github.com/Megvii-BaseDetection/YOLOX/tree/0.1.0">model zoo</a>. After downloading the pretrained models, you can put them under &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;/pretrained.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Train ablation model (MOT17 half train and CrowdHuman)</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Train MOT17 test model (MOT17 train, CrowdHuman, Cityperson and ETHZ)</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_det.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_det.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Train MOT20 test model (MOT20 train, CrowdHuman)</strong></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">For MOT20, you need to clip the bounding boxes inside the image.</p>
<p dir="auto">Add clip operation in <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/72cd6dd24083c337a9177e484b12bb2b5b3069a6/yolox/data/data_augment.py#L134">line 134-135 in data_augment.py</a>, <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/72cd6dd24083c337a9177e484b12bb2b5b3069a6/yolox/data/datasets/mosaicdetection.py#L122">line 122-125 in mosaicdetection.py</a>, <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/72cd6dd24083c337a9177e484b12bb2b5b3069a6/yolox/data/datasets/mosaicdetection.py#L217">line 217-225 in mosaicdetection.py</a>, <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/72cd6dd24083c337a9177e484b12bb2b5b3069a6/yolox/utils/boxes.py#L115">line 115-118 in boxes.py</a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_mot20_ch.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_mot20_ch.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Train custom dataset</strong></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">First, you need to prepare your dataset in COCO format. You can refer to <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/tools/convert_mot17_to_coco.py">MOT-to-COCO</a> or <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/tools/convert_crowdhuman_to_coco.py">CrowdHuman-to-COCO</a>. Then, you need to create a Exp file for your dataset. You can refer to the <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ch.py">CrowdHuman</a> training Exp file. Don't forget to modify get_data_loader() and get_eval_loader in your Exp file. Finally, you can train bytetrack on your dataset by running:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/your_exp_file.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/train.py -f exps/example/mot/your_exp_file.py -d 8 -b 48 --fp16 -o -c pretrained/yolox_x.pth</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tracking</h2><a id="user-content-tracking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tracking" href="#tracking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Evaluation on MOT17 half val</strong></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Run ByteTrack:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/track.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/track.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can get 76.6 MOTA using our pretrained model.</p>
<p dir="auto">Run other trackers:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python3 tools/track_sort.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse
python3 tools/track_deepsort.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse
python3 tools/track_motdt.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse"><pre>python3 tools/track_sort.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse
python3 tools/track_deepsort.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse
python3 tools/track_motdt.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_ablation.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_ablation.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Test on MOT17</strong></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Run ByteTrack:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/track.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_det.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_x_mot17.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse
python3 tools/interpolation.py"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/track.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_det.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_x_mot17.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse
python3 tools/interpolation.py</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Submit the txt files to <a href="https://motchallenge.net/" rel="nofollow">MOTChallenge</a> website and you can get 79+ MOTA (For 80+ MOTA, you need to carefully tune the test image size and high score detection threshold of each sequence).</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Test on MOT20</strong></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">We use the input size 1600 x 896 for MOT20-04, MOT20-07 and 1920 x 736 for MOT20-06, MOT20-08. You can edit it in <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_mot20_ch.py">yolox_x_mix_mot20_ch.py</a></p>
<p dir="auto">Run ByteTrack:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/track.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_mot20_ch.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_x_mot20.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse --match_thresh 0.7 --mot20
python3 tools/interpolation.py"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/track.py -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_mot20_ch.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_x_mot20.pth.tar -b 1 -d 1 --fp16 --fuse --match_thresh 0.7 --mot20
python3 tools/interpolation.py</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Submit the txt files to <a href="https://motchallenge.net/" rel="nofollow">MOTChallenge</a> website and you can get 77+ MOTA (For higher MOTA, you need to carefully tune the test image size and high score detection threshold of each sequence).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Applying BYTE to other trackers</h2><a id="user-content-applying-byte-to-other-trackers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Applying BYTE to other trackers" href="#applying-byte-to-other-trackers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">See <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/tree/main/tutorials">tutorials</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Combining BYTE with other detectors</h2><a id="user-content-combining-byte-with-other-detectors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Combining BYTE with other detectors" href="#combining-byte-with-other-detectors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Suppose you have already got the detection results 'dets' (x1, y1, x2, y2, score) from other detectors, you can simply pass the detection results to BYTETracker (you need to first modify some post-processing code according to the format of your detection results in <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/yolox/tracker/byte_tracker.py">byte_tracker.py</a>):</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from yolox.tracker.byte_tracker import BYTETracker
tracker = BYTETracker(args)
for image in images:
   dets = detector(image)
   online_targets = tracker.update(dets, info_imgs, img_size)"><pre class="notranslate"><code>from yolox.tracker.byte_tracker import BYTETracker
tracker = BYTETracker(args)
for image in images:
   dets = detector(image)
   online_targets = tracker.update(dets, info_imgs, img_size)
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can get the tracking results in each frame from 'online_targets'. You can refer to <a href="https://github.com/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/yolox/evaluators/mot_evaluator.py">mot_evaluators.py</a> to pass the detection results to BYTETracker.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Demo</h2><a id="user-content-demo" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Demo" href="#demo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ifzhang/ByteTrack/blob/main/assets/palace_demo.gif"><img src="/ifzhang/ByteTrack/raw/main/assets/palace_demo.gif" width="600" data-animated-image="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd &lt;ByteTrack_HOME&gt;
python3 tools/demo_track.py video -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_det.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_x_mot17.pth.tar --fp16 --fuse --save_result"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>ByteTrack_HOME<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
python3 tools/demo_track.py video -f exps/example/mot/yolox_x_mix_det.py -c pretrained/bytetrack_x_mot17.pth.tar --fp16 --fuse --save_result</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Deploy</h2><a id="user-content-deploy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Deploy" href="#deploy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

  </cookie-consent-link>
</li>

      </ul>
    </nav>
  </div>
